                                                    Preface


      The Procurement Programs (P-1) exhibit is derived from and consistent with the Next Generation
Resource Management System database.
      The P-1 is provided annually to the DoW oversight committees of the Congress coincident with the
transmittal of the President's Budget. This document is also provided to Office of Assistance Secretary of
War (Public Affairs) for use by non-DoW activities, and is available to the public on the Internet at
https://comptroller.defense.gov/.


                          Office of the Under Secretary of War (Comptroller)




     Preparation of the P-1 cost the Department of War a total of approximately $40,000 in FY 2026.
                                              (RefID: 1-055B707)
